2024-12-17T03:58:12Z #11 173.0

2024-12-17T03:58:12Z #11 173.0 
2024-12-17T03:58:12Z #11 173.0 
2024-12-17T03:58:12Z #11 173.0 To enable CUDA support, please follow UCX's instruction above.
2024-12-17T03:58:12Z #11 173.0 
2024-12-17T03:58:12Z #11 173.0 To additionally enable NCCL support, run:    conda install nccl
2024-12-17T03:58:12Z #11 173.0 
2024-12-17T03:58:12Z #11 173.0 
2024-12-17T03:58:12Z #11 173.0 On Linux, Open MPI is built with CUDA awareness but it is disabled by default.
2024-12-17T03:58:12Z #11 173.0 To enable it, please set the environment variable
2024-12-17T03:58:12Z #11 173.0 OMPI_MCA_opal_cuda_support=true
2024-12-17T03:58:12Z #11 173.0 before launching your MPI processes.
2024-12-17T03:58:12Z #11 173.0 Equivalently, you can set the MCA parameter in the command line:
2024-12-17T03:58:12Z #11 173.0 mpiexec --mca opal_cuda_support 1 ...
2024-12-17T03:58:12Z #11 173.0 Note that you might also need to set UCX_MEMTYPE_CACHE=n for CUDA awareness via
2024-12-17T03:58:12Z #11 173.0 UCX. Please consult UCX documentation for further details.
